## 1. [Class (1983)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/class-1983?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=class-1983&utm_term=class-1983)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/class-1983?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=class-1983&amp;utm_term=class-1983"><img alt="class-tt0085346-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/class-tt0085346-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Class" (1983) is a captivating coming-of-age story that seamlessly blends elements of drama, comedy, and romance. Narrative genius Rob Lowe stars as Jonathan "Jon" Wellington III, a young man navigating the tumultuous terrain of high school life at an esteemed private institution. His otherwise ordinary existence takes a wild turn after a night of debauchery, where he encounters the alluring Jacqueline Bisset. Unbeknownst to him, their unforgettable encounter will leave him with memories he may never forget and an intriguing story still to unfold. Directed by Lewis John Carlino and co-written by Jim Kouf and David Greenwalt, "Class" transports the audience into the high-stakes world of adolescent life, where passions are intense, hearts are vulnerable, and friendships are tested. The film also features impressive performances from its supporting cast, including Andrew McCarthy, who plays a key role in Jon's journey throughout this unpredictable narrative arc. "Class" was met with an R rating for its explicit themes and sexual content, which adds further weight to its compelling storyline and delivers an enthralling cinematic experience. The 1983 box office performance exceeded expectations with a gross of over $21 million, showcasing the film's commercial success alongside its critical acclaim. In an entertaining ensemble of familiar stars and talented unknowns, "Class" delivers a compelling message about the sometimes blurred lines between youthful rebellion and genuine love. As Jon unravels the complexities of his newfound relationships, he learns more about himself and the unpredictable world he inhabits. A must-watch for fans of coming-of-age cinema, "Class" stands as an enduring monument to the power of storytelling and an unforgettable account of timeless themes. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Drama, Romance
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 38min
- Directed by: Lewis John Carlino
- Starring: Jacqueline Bisset, Rob Lowe, Andrew McCarthy
- Box Office:
 - Budget: $7,000,000 (estimated)

## 2. [Grandview, U.S.A. (1984)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/grandview-u-s-a-1984?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=grandview-u-s-a-1984&utm_term=grandview-usa-1984)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/grandview-u-s-a-1984?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=grandview-u-s-a-1984&amp;utm_term=grandview-usa-1984"><img alt="grandview-u-s-a--tt0087359-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/grandview-u-s-a--tt0087359-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Grandview, U. S. A. " is a 1984 drama film set in the small town of Grandview. The story centers on a young man, desperate to break free from his father's oppressive rule and his mundane scholarship, to pursue his passion for oceanography. As he inches closer to his high school graduation, he faces the dilemma of whether he is ready to spread his wings and leave the comfort of his small town life behind. The film boasts powerful performances from a star-studded cast including Jamie Lee Curtis, C. Thomas Howell and Patrick Swayze, under the direction of Randal Kleiser. It's an authentic portrayal of teenage rebellion and dreams, filled with moments of drama, passion, and Americana. Whether you're a fan of coming-of-age stories or simply looking for a nostalgic trip down memory lane, "Grandview, U. S. A. " is sure to captivate with its engaging narrative and compelling performances. 



<br>

- Genres: Drama
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 37min
- Directed by: Randal Kleiser
- Starring: Jamie Lee Curtis, C. Thomas Howell, Patrick Swayze
- Box Office:
 - Gross USA: $4,743,119
 - Opening Weekend USA: $2,194,293
 - Cumulative Worldwide Gross: $4,743,119
- IMDb Rating: 5.5

## 3. [Sixteen Candles (1984)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/sixteen-candles-1984?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=sixteen-candles-1984&utm_term=sixteen-candles-1984)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/sixteen-candles-1984?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=sixteen-candles-1984&amp;utm_term=sixteen-candles-1984"><img alt="sixteen-candles-tt0088128-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/sixteen-candles-tt0088128-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Sixteen Candles" (1984) is a coming-of-age comedy directed by John Hughes, starring Molly Ringwald, Anthony Michael Hall, and Justin Henry. The film follows the story of Samantha, a high school teenager whose sweet sixteen birthday takes a disastrously awkward turn when her entire family forgets about it. Embarrassed and ignored, Samantha navigates the challenges of adolescence, friendships, and love amidst a whirlwind of humorous and unexpected adventures. Packed with teenage drama, romance, and comedy, this classic 80s movie is a must-watch for fans of the genre. 



<br>

## 4. [Better Off Dead... (1985)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/better-off-dead-1985?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=better-off-dead-1985&utm_term=better-off-dead-1985)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/better-off-dead-1985?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=better-off-dead-1985&amp;utm_term=better-off-dead-1985"><img alt="better-off-dead--tt0088794-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/better-off-dead--tt0088794-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Better Off Dead" (1985) is a wacky teen comedy that tells the story of Lane, a high schooler who resorts to increasingly absurd suicide attempts after being dumped by his girlfriend. As his attempts fail, Lane finds himself wrapped up in wild and outrageous nightmares. Featuring John Cusack in the leading role, this film combines teenage drama with outrageous scenarios that keep you captivated and laughing. Watch Lane struggle to navigate the challenges of high school, awkward relationships, and a quirky French exchange student, with a healthy dose of skiing antics on the side. "Better Off Dead" boasts a unique blend of comedy and romance that has garnered an IMDb rating of 7.1 and captivated audiences for decades. Embedded with wild and unpredictable moments, this movie will keep viewers engaged and entertained throughout its entire 97-minute runtime. The film is directed by the talented Savage Steve Holland, who not only directs but also writes this captivating story. Sharing the screen with Cusack are David Ogden Stiers and Kim Darby, all contributing to the overall charm and appeal of "Better Off Dead. "

For fans of teen dramas and comedy, "Better Off Dead" is a must-watch film that offers hours of entertainment and ample opportunities to escape from reality right along with its lovable protagonist, Lane. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Romance
- Rated: PG
- Runtime: 1h 37min
- Directed by: Savage Steve Holland
- Starring: John Cusack, David Ogden Stiers, Kim Darby
- Box Office:

## 5. [The Sure Thing (1985)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-sure-thing-1985?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-sure-thing-1985&utm_term=the-sure-thing-1985)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-sure-thing-1985?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=the-sure-thing-1985&amp;utm_term=the-sure-thing-1985"><img alt="the-sure-thing-tt0090103-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/the-sure-thing-tt0090103-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"The Sure Thing" is a compelling, coming-of-age comedy-drama that will strike a chord with anyone who has ever been young, foolish, and optimistic. Set in 1985, the film follows the journey of Walter Gibson, a college freshman and a university student facing a dry spell in his love life. His long-time friend sets him up with some sure-fire action on the West Coast, but his plans are thrown off course when he's paired with his classmate Allison for a cross-country road trip. Directed by Rob Reiner and starring John Cusack, Daphne Zuniga, and Anthony Edwards, "The Sure Thing" is a rollercoaster of romance, youthful rebellion, and self-discovery. As Gibson and Allison navigate the American highway system through hitchhiking, misadventures, and mishaps, they start to see each other in a new light, forcing them to confront their growing feelings and past misunderstandings. With elements of hitchhiking, one-night stands, and clumsy sex in college dorm rooms, "The Sure Thing" delicately balances between comedy and drama, offering a thought-provoking exploration into the complexities of youth and desire. This charming classic has been compared to other esteemed films such as "One Crazy Summer, " "Say Anything, " and "Better Off Dead, " making it a must-watch for fans of coming-of-age tales. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy, Drama, Romance
- Rated: PG-13
- Runtime: 1h 35min
- Directed by: Rob Reiner
- Starring: John Cusack, Daphne Zuniga, Anthony Edwards
- Box Office:

## 6. [The Journey of Natty Gann (1985)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-journey-of-natty-gann-1985?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=the-journey-of-natty-gann-1985&utm_term=the-journey-of-natty-gann-1985)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/the-journey-of-natty-gann-1985?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=the-journey-of-natty-gann-1985&amp;utm_term=the-journey-of-natty-gann-1985"><img alt="the-journey-of-natty-gann-tt0089385-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/the-journey-of-natty-gann-tt0089385-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"The Journey of Natty Gann" is a captivating tale from the 1980s that takes viewers on a heartwarming adventure during the Great Depression. Set in the mid-1930s, the film follows a feisty tomboy named Natty Gann who embarks on a daring journey to join her single father, who is 2,000 miles away and working. Along the way, she faces challenges, makes new friends, and even bonds with a wild wolf. Packed with adventure, drama, and a touch of early 20th-century American history, this family-oriented movie, released in 1985, provides an unforgettable story that teaches the importance of courage, determination, and love. With notable performances by Meredith Salenger, John Cusack, and Jed, and directed by Jeremy Kagan, "The Journey of Natty Gann" is a must-watch film that's perfect for all ages.

## 7. [One Crazy Summer (1986)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/one-crazy-summer-1986?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=one-crazy-summer-1986&utm_term=one-crazy-summer-1986)

<br>

"One Crazy Summer" is a refreshing 1986 comedy that will keep you entertained with its clever plot and engaging characters. The film follows an ambitious teenage cartoonist and his group of friends as they embark on a mission to save a talented singer's family property from being snatched up by greedy developers. As they navigate the challenges of the season, they uncover a long-standing family feud and a dastardly villain. The movie masterfully blends heartwarming romance with hilarious antics, making it a perfect choice for a fun-filled summer evening. With an outstanding cast led by John Cusack and Demi Moore, "One Crazy Summer" promises a memorable cinematic experience as you join its lovable characters on their unforgettable adventure.

## 8. [Stand by Me (1986)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/stand-by-me-1986?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=stand-by-me-1986&utm_term=stand-by-me-1986)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/stand-by-me-1986?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=stand-by-me-1986&amp;utm_term=stand-by-me-1986"><img alt="stand-by-me-tt0092005-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/stand-by-me-tt0092005-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Stand by Me" is a timeless coming-of-age adventure that transports audiences back to the halcyon days of '50s America. Directed by Rob Reiner and adapted from Stephen King's novella, the film follows a group of young boys on a trek through the Oregon wilderness. Their mission: to find the body of a missing boy. Along the way, the boys come face-to-face with the realities of growing up, navigating friendship, loss, and the harsh truths of life. The stellar cast, led by Wil Wheaton, River Phoenix, and Corey Feldman, delivers compelling performances that breathe life into this nostalgic tale. As the boys bond over shared experiences and secrets, their journey becomes a poignant exploration of childhood innocence and the inevitable passage into adulthood. This R-rated drama boasts a runtime of 1h 29min and is lauded for its exceptional storytelling, unforgettable performances, and poignant themes, earning it a well-deserved spot at #228 on the top-rated movies list. It has been nominated for an Academy Award and has won several accolades, including six wins and twelve nominations. Set in the idyllic backdrop of the American countryside, "Stand by Me" captures the essence of youth and the enduring power of friendship. It is a must-watch for fans of adventure, comedy, and drama, with comparisons to other cinematic classics like "Groundhog Day, " "Dead Poets Society, " and "Rocky. "



<br>

## 9. [Hot Pursuit (1987)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/hot-pursuit-1987?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=hot-pursuit-1987&utm_term=hot-pursuit-1987)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/hot-pursuit-1987?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=hot-pursuit-1987&amp;utm_term=hot-pursuit-1987"><img alt="hot-pursuit-tt0093215-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/hot-pursuit-tt0093215-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Hot Pursuit" is a hilarious 1987 comedy that follows the misadventures of Dan, a hopelessly devoted boyfriend, as he tries to reunite with his girlfriend in the Caribbean. After missing their flight, Dan embarks on a wild journey, navigating through a series of offbeat characters including friendly locals, a suspicious yacht captain, corrupt police, and even pirates. The film boasts an all-star cast including John Cusack, Robert Loggia, and Jerry Stiller, and is directed by Steven Lisberger. With a perfect blend of action, romance, and humor, "Hot Pursuit" will leave you laugh out loud and eager for more of its unpredictable and entertaining twists & turns. 



<br>

- Genres: Comedy
- Rated: PG-13
- Runtime: 1h 33min
- Directed by: Steven Lisberger
- Starring: John Cusack, Robert Loggia, Jerry Stiller
- Box Office:
 - Budget: $7,000,000 (estimated)
 - Gross USA: $4,215,849
 - Opening Weekend USA: $1,507,645
 - Cumulative Worldwide Gross: $4,215,849

The movie is a blend of comedy and drama, weaving together elements of satire and mockumentary to create a distinctively engaging viewing experience. The movie chronicles a touching love story that spans over 30 years, from 1931 to 1965, set against the contrasting backdrops of the Arctic and World War II. The story unfolds with a young Avik, an Eskimo boy with tuberculosis, being transported to a hospital in Montreal. Here he encounters Albertine, a beautiful woman he later meets again when he enlists in World War II, leading to a passionate love story. Directed by Vincent Ward and written by Louis Nowra and Ward, "Map of the Human Heart" is a powerful statement on love, identity, and perseverance, with its plot structure reminiscent of a classic map. The well-crafted performances of stars Jason Scott Lee, Anne Parillaud, and Patrick Bergin are a testament to the high-quality storytelling. With its breathtaking setting and engaging narrative, this film leaves an indelible impression on the audience. The movie is a must-watch for fans of adventure, drama, and romance, and is highly recommended for viewers who enjoy a unique take on love stories.

"The Player" is a gripping 1992 crime-drama that combines elements of comedy to tell an intriguing tale within the world of Hollywood. With an "R" content rating, this 2-hour film masterfully incorporates a long take, tracking shots, and male frontal nudity to deliver an intense experience. The protagonist is a high-ranking studio executive, portrayed by Tim Robbins, who receives death threats from a mysterious scriptwriter whose work he has rejected, keeping audiences on edge as they try to guess which script poses the menacing danger. Beyond its captivating plot, "The Player" is a notable film in the comedy, crime, and drama genres, receiving nominations for three Oscars and being directed by the legendary Robert Altman. The story unfurls against the backdrop of the film industry, showcasing a stark behind-the-scenes glimpse of a film studio. Intriguing performances are delivered by other notable cast members, including Greta Scacchi and Fred Ward. "The Player" was produced under a combination of independent and major production companies including Avenue Pictures, Spelling Entertainment, and Addis Wechsler Pictures. The film was released in the U. S. on May 8, 1992, grossing $21.7 million worldwide against an estimated budget of $8 million. It garnered favorable ratings from both critics and audiences, as evidenced by its 7.5 IMDb rating based on over 64,000 votes. Fans of movies exploring themes in the film industry, tracking shots, or featuring ensemble casts will find "The Player" a compelling and entertaining choice. ## 27. [Floundering (1994)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/floundering-1994?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=floundering-1994&utm_term=floundering-1994)

"Floundering" is a 1994 comedic drama set in post-riot Los Angeles. The story revolves around John Boyz, a floundering thirty-something unemployed man living on Venice Beach, who's caught in a loop of trying to figure out his life's purpose. Despite his desire to help people, he remains trapped by his lack of motivation. The film masterfully paints a vivid picture of unemployment and societal malaise in the 1990s, accentuated by the backdrop of Venice California and Los Angeles. The movie features a stellar performance by James Le Gros in the lead role, supported by a talented ensemble including Shaka Zulu and Zander Schloss. It is a raw, witty, and engaging exploration of the human condition, with director Peter McCarthy, along with writers Jo Harvey Allen and John Cusack, crafting an authentic and compelling narrative. For those who appreciate thought-provoking comedies mixed with elements of drama, "Floundering" offers an insightful and entertaining exploration of life's uncertainties. Its themes of unemployment, societal issues, and personal struggle continue to resonate today and make it a compelling watch for anyone interested in these evocative subjects. The film was released by Front Films and was a commercial failure, grossing only $20,031 worldwide. Despite this, "Floundering" received one award nomination and has been compared by IMDb users to similar movies like "Money for Nothing" and "Beautiful Girls".

## 36. [Midnight in the Garden of Good and Evil (1997)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/midnight-in-the-garden-of-good-and-evil-1997?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=midnight-in-the-garden-of-good-and-evil-1997&utm_term=midnight-in-the-garden-of-good-and-evil-1997)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/midnight-in-the-garden-of-good-and-evil-1997?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=midnight-in-the-garden-of-good-and-evil-1997&amp;utm_term=midnight-in-the-garden-of-good-and-evil-1997"><img alt="midnight-in-the-garden-of-good-and-evil-tt0119668-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/midnight-in-the-garden-of-good-and-evil-tt0119668-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Midnight in the Garden of Good and Evil" is a gripping crime-drama from 1997, directed by the legendary Clint Eastwood and based on the true story of a millionaire's murder trial, as presented by a city reporter who gets uniquely involved in the case. The story unfolds in the vivid and enigmatic setting of Savannah, Georgia, delving deep into themes of good and evil, morality and law, as it portrays the unlikely friendship that develops between the reporter and the accused millionaire. The movie stars John Cusack as the city reporter, and the talented Kevin Spacey as the charismatic millionaire. Their evolving relationship imparts a fascinating depth to the narrative, which is enhanced by a supporting cast of notable actors like Jack Thompson. The screenplay, adapted from John Berendt's novel of the same name, masterfully intertwines the elements of crime, drama, and mystery with a deep sense of intrigue. As the American forces fight valiantly against the Japanese, the film offers a powerful, character-driven narrative through the eyes of soldiers grappling with the horrors and complexities of war. With an impressive ensemble cast led by Jim Caviezel, Sean Penn, and Nick Nolte, the movie captures the spirit of camaraderie, bravery, and sacrifice that define a nation at war. Set against the backdrop of dense jungles and towering hills, "The Thin Red Line" delivers a visceral and immersive portrayal of battle, earning itself numerous awards and nominations. Its poetic cinematography, evocative score, and thought-provoking script combine to create a haunting, unforgettable masterpiece that transcends the war genre. Experience the powerful storytelling of Terrence Malick in this unforgettable film, sure to resonate with audiences for generations to come.

## 54. [Max (2002)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/max-2002?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=max-2002&utm_term=max-2002)

<br>

"Max" (2002) is a compelling drama that delves into the complex friendship between an art dealer, played by John Cusack, and his student, Adolf Hitler. Set in 1918, this gripping film offers a unique perspective on the early life of the infamous dictator, focusing on his passion for painting and his relationships with those around him. The story follows Rothman, a sophisticated art dealer, who discovers a genius painter named Adolf. As they build an unconventional friendship, Rothman's mistress, a Jewish woman, adds another layer of intrigue to the tale. As Europe enters a tumultuous period, the lives of these characters become increasingly intertwined, and their choices have far-reaching consequences. Directed and written by Menno Meyjes, "Max" boasts striking performances by John Cusack, Noah Taylor, and Leelee Sobieski. The captivating story and powerful acting earned the film multiple nominations and awards, making it a must-watch for fans of historical dramas. ## 100. [Citizenfour (2014)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/citizenfour-2014?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=citizenfour-2014&utm_term=citizenfour-2014)

<br>

"Citizenfour" is a gripping documentary that offers a rare and shocking glimpse into the world of mass surveillance. Directed by Laura Poitras, the film delves beneath the surface of government intrusion, focusing on the life-changing revelations of Edward Snowden, a former NSA contractor. Teaming up with documentarian Laura Poitras and journalist Glenn Greenwald, Snowden decides to expose the scope of mass surveillance techniques adopted by government agencies like NSA. Filled with suspense and intrigue, "Citizenfour" captures the tense Hong Kong meetings between Snowden, Greenwald, and Poitras culminating in Snowden's unprecedented disclosure of classified information. Revealed are alarming practices of government surveillance that span across nations, prompting heated debates around privacy rights, government transparency, and espionage. Delivering a thought-provoking narrative, "Citizenfour" has won worldwide acclaim, including an Academy Award, making it an essential viewing for anyone interested in understanding the complexities of government surveillance in the digital age. 



<br>

- Genres: Documentary, Biography
- Rated: R
- Runtime: 1h 54min
- Directed by: Laura Poitras
- Starring: Edward Snowden, Glenn Greenwald, William Binney
- Box Office:
 - Gross USA: $2,800,870
 - Opening Weekend USA: $126,321
 - Cumulative Worldwide Gross: $3,780,692
- IMDb Rating: 8.0
- Awards: Won 1 Oscar, 44 wins & 39 nominations total

This is not just any war film; it is a vivid portrayal of the harsh realities that haunt the streets of America's third-largest city. "Chi-Raq" has been recognized for its compelling storytelling and exceptional performances, earning several awards and nominations. With a runtime of just two hours, this film will keep you engaged and thinking long after the credits roll. ## 119. [Disclosure (2020)](https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/disclosure-2020?utm_source=serp.media&utm_medium=website&utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&utm_content=disclosure-2020&utm_term=disclosure-2020)

<div class="image"><a href="https://serp.ly/@serpmovies/amazon/disclosure-2020?utm_source=serp.media&amp;utm_medium=website&amp;utm_campaign=%40serpmedia&amp;utm_content=disclosure-2020&amp;utm_term=disclosure-2020"><img alt="disclosure-tt8637504-1" src="https://imagedelivery.net/vy2bglCGN6hEeWOnSe2c7A/disclosure-tt8637504-1/h=600"/></a></div>

<br>

"Disclosure" delves into the intricate relationship between Hollywood's portrayal of transgender individuals and their real-life impact on American culture. This compelling documentary, directed by Sam Feder and starring Laverne Cox, Bianca Leigh, and Jen Richards, provides an in-depth look at the history of transgender representation in film and television. It reflects on the power of storytelling to shape societal perceptions, discussing the importance of authentic, nuanced narratives in shaping societal discourse. Through a blend of interviews, film clips, and expert commentary, "Disclosure" takes us on a fascinating journey through the evolving landscape of transgender media representation. It examines the evolution of this representation, from early, stereotyped portrayals to the more complex, humanized depictions of today. The film also delves into the consequences of these representations on the lives and experiences of transgender individuals, offering a sobering yet ultimately hopeful exploration of the power of storytelling. Award-winning and thought-provoking, "Disclosure" is a must-watch for anyone interested in the intersection of media, culture, and societal attitudes towards transgender individuals. With its blend of compelling narrative and insightful commentary, this documentary offers a fresh, eye-opening perspective on an often-misunderstood topic.
